    function readConsentSettingCookie(cookie) {
    let consentSettings = "{}";
    const parts = ("; " + cookie).split("; consentSettings=");
    if (parts.length === 2) {
        const element = parts.pop();
        if (element !== undefined) {

                consentSettings = value;
            }
        }
    }
    return consentSettings;
}
